Okada Hosts Foreign Reporters to Explain Naval Disarmament Attitude 24

Opposes Current Ratio Principle

Conducts Conciliatory Diplomacy with the United States

(Tokyo) - At 2:30 this afternoon, Prime Minister Okada hosted 20 foreign news and communication reporters at his official residence for the first time, reading the following statement: The current government's foreign policy has been clearly stated in the imperial rescript and policy outline of March 27 last year. Its fundamental policy is to seek world peace. Now that various countries are experiencing fluctuations in politics, economy, and ideology, and international relations are also experiencing unrest, we must use various means to restore international relations and maintain peace. Although "Manchukuo" has only been established for two years, its sound development is truly commendable. The Empire has always provided full assistance and intends to continue to provide assistance in the future. The turmoil in China has a significant impact on the political situation in East Asia, so the Empire is most concerned about it. The relationship with Soviet Russia should be carefully considered. At present, there are no pending issues with the United States, and a traditional friendly relationship is maintained with Britain. However, commercial disputes have arisen everywhere recently, but they can be adjusted with a spirit of mutual concession. We are a nation that is progressing day by day, so we strive to maintain, enhance, and improve friendly relations with other countries. If other countries fully recognize the Empire's position in East Asia and understand its ability to pacify East Asia and promote peace, then the various issues in East Asia and the naval issue will not be difficult to resolve, and we believe that we can contribute to the promotion of world peace. (31st Dentsu Telegram)

(Tokyo) - After Prime Minister Okada met with foreign reporters today and read the statement, he answered questions from the foreign reporters. First, Repp, the representative of the United Press, questioned the opinion on the naval issue. Prime Minister Okada replied that the armaments of various countries should be limited to the minimum extent. True disarmament should be carried out by countries with the strongest military equipment limiting their military equipment. The reporter asked if Japan's claim to abandon the ratio means shrinking the British and American navies to the level of Japan. The Prime Minister replied that this was not the intention. In principle, we cannot agree with the current ratio, but we do not expect rapid changes. The reporter asked if there was an intention to abandon the Washington Treaty. The Prime Minister replied that whether to abandon it or not is currently under study. The reporter asked if they were dissatisfied with the ratio, then what methods were there for disarmament. The Prime Minister replied that other appropriate methods could be found, but now was not the time to speak clearly. The reporter asked if Japan hopes for success at the next disarmament conference. The Prime Minister replied that he personally hopes for success. Even if it breaks down, Japan and the United States will not compete to build warships afterwards. The reporter asked if President Roosevelt's visit to Hawaii was related to strengthening the naval base. The Prime Minister replied that if no actual problems occur, then it is impossible to know. The reporter asked whether maintaining the South Seas Mandate Territory was more important for military or commercial reasons. The Prime Minister replied that from the perspective of investment and other relations, commerce should be more important. The reporter asked about the Prime Minister's views on Japan-US relations. The Prime Minister replied that Japan and the United States must always maintain friendly relations. (31st Dentsu Telegram)

(30th Havas Telegram)

Austrian Capital Incident: Two Main Culprits Executed by Hanging 30

Bloody Shirt Serves as Evidence, Viewers Moved to Compassion

Vienna: Today, the trial of the murderers of Dr. Dollfuss continued. The undershirt worn by Dr. Dollfuss on the day of his assassination was presented as evidence in court. Part of the shirt was stained with blood, and the stiff collar was blackened by gunpowder residue. The sight moved everyone. Experts testified that the muzzle of the gun was at least eight inches away from Dr. Dollfuss when fired. After being shot, his arms and legs were paralyzed. Even with medical assistance, his life could not be extended beyond two hours. Furthermore, police inspector Stanberger claimed that he had requested both a doctor and a priest for Dr. Dollfuss, but the family doctor could not be reached immediately, and the telephone line was cut, so a priest could not be invited either. Stanberger stated that he was not in the room when Dr. Dollfuss was shot and suddenly felt weak, so he was carried out of the courtroom. After all the witnesses testified, the judges determined that defendants Panneta and Hollswebach were indeed guilty of murdering Dr. Dollfuss and sentenced them to death by hanging. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Vienna: After hearing the verdict, Panneta said that he had fulfilled his duty to the country. Hollswebach told the court that he had participated in the rebellion because he heard that a new government had been established without bloodshed and was willing to accept the consequences of his actions. The defendants' lawyers pleaded for exemption from punishment in the name of National Socialism, claiming that the new Austrian constitution was illegal. They are now petitioning President Miklas for clemency. Continued report: The petition for clemency has been rejected by the president, and the two criminals have been executed by firing squad. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Vienna: National Socialist Party members Panneta and Hollswebach, accused of shooting and killing Prime Minister Dollfuss, were tried by a special military tribunal this afternoon. The courthouse was heavily guarded, and no unauthorized persons were allowed inside. When the defendants arrived, they were escorted by military police. Both were wearing ordinary clothes, and their shoelaces had been removed to prevent suicide. Both were accused of firing one shot each at Dr. Dollfuss. According to the prosecutor's opening statement, neither of the bullets fired by the two defendants were fatal. Dr. Dollfuss died from excessive blood loss due to a lack of medical attention after being wounded.

Defendant Panneta testified that before their rebellion, someone had told them that certain high-ranking officials would provide protection and instructed them not to shed blood unless absolutely necessary for self-defense. He had entered a dark room in the Prime Minister's office and ordered a robust man, likely Major Fey, to raise his hands. He suddenly felt someone touch his right arm and noticed that there was another person in the room, who was Dr. Dollfuss. He personally saw Dr. Dollfuss fall to the ground and heard him say, "I yield my position to Rintelen."

When asked why he entered the Prime Minister's office, Panneta replied that he wanted to detain all the cabinet members and inquire about the reason for this. Panneta did not answer. Panneta continued to testify that after they were captured in the Prime Minister's office, Vienna Deputy Police Chief Stuher gave a speech to the crowd, saying that if the murderers of Dr. Dollfuss confessed, the rest would be freed. Panneta was very indignant because he had confessed, but none of his comrades were freed. Stuher then testified that he had promised freedom to the rebels who were not involved in the murder of Prime Minister Dollfuss and former army and police personnel.

Hollswebach, accused of treason, mentioned in his testimony an unknown, strange person who ordered him to arrest the cabinet members, saying that this person issued the order in the name of the Federal President. "I complied," he said.

When Major Fey testified in court, security was increased. Fey admitted that he had told Hollswebach that if the rebels released the hostages, they would be granted freedom, given safe passage, sent to the German border, and promised that his words would be kept.

Minister of Social Welfare Stuermer also testified, admitting that he knew that after Dr. Dollfuss's death, he had still agreed to grant safe passage to the rebels. However, he later heard that Prime Minister Dollfuss had been murdered, not fatally wounded in mutual combat, so he felt that the situation was different from before. "I am a soldier and respect my word. However, whether the murder of Prime Minister Dollfuss was the act of a soldier or a coward, and whether this murder was a despicable conspiracy, I am willing to let the court decide," he said.

At this point, the defendants' lawyer pleaded exhaustion and requested an adjournment. The court rejected the request, and the defendants' lawyer announced his withdrawal from the court, forcing the court to continue the trial tomorrow. The court said it would punish the lawyer and rejected the lawyer's request to subpoena former German ambassador to Austria, Dr. Rieth, and the new Prime Minister, Schuschnigg, to testify. The defendants' lawyer also requested that the indictment for assassination be revised, but this was also rejected.

According to reports, Panneta's wife said she wanted to visit Mrs. Dollfuss and that she missed Mrs. Dollfuss and her children very much. Mrs. Dollfuss would certainly not blame her. The last time she saw her husband was on July 24th, when he was wearing a bathrobe and said he was going swimming. (Reuters dispatch, 30th)

Vienna: The cabinet held a special meeting last night and issued an order that the property of all those who participated in the National Socialist rebellion would be confiscated. Those with minor involvement would be detained in concentration camps and sentenced to hard labor. The cabinet also listened to the report of the Minister of Defense, who said that national security had been restored and the rebels' last attempt had failed. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Security Restored in Austria 31

While Starhemberg's Real Power Expands

Lack of Qualifications Prevents Immediate Appointment as Prime Minister

Vienna: Military police are still on strict alert throughout Austria today, but the situation seems very calm. The international tension has also eased somewhat since the formal announcement last night that Foreign Minister Tauschnitz has been transferred to the post of ambassador to Germany. Vice-Chancellor Prince Starhemberg has also resumed his position as commander of the "Patriotic Front" today. This unit was originally part of Dollfuss's old guard and has exclusive rights to the term "Patriotic." Key government positions are also monopolized by members of this unit. (National Telegraph, 31st)

(Paris): The formation of the Schuschnigg cabinet in Austria was swift and has been met with satisfaction by various newspapers here. They believe that Schuschnigg will be able to complete Dollfuss's unfinished business. While the new cabinet may face dangers, it will certainly lead to an obvious improvement in the international political situation. L'Écho de Paris reported, "Schuschnigg's personality and his relationship with the late Prime Minister Dollfuss are clear evidence that the new cabinet will follow in his footsteps." Le Petit Parisien reported, "The new government's resolute determination not to allow Germany to use underhanded tricks to interfere in Austrian internal affairs is enough to make the countries responsible for guaranteeing Austria's independence feel sympathetic and willing to help." (Havas dispatch, 31st)

(London): London correspondents in Vienna report that Austria is once again in the midst of a rapidly brewing coup. Since Minister of Education Schuschnigg was appointed Federal Chancellor, the Heimwehr has unanimously clamored for Prince Starhemberg to succeed Dollfuss as Federal Chancellor and for the two advisors to the Federal Chancellor to also be members of the Heimwehr. According to reports from Vienna, a state of emergency was declared twice yesterday. Government offices were heavily guarded by military police, as if facing a major enemy, and the Heimwehr headquarters were surrounded by three lines of defense. London's public opinion is very satisfied with Schuschnigg's appointment as Federal Chancellor, as it believes that Prince Starhemberg's political qualifications have not yet been established and that he lacks diplomatic experience. (National Telegraph, 30th)

(Paris): A correspondent for the Paris Morning Post in Vienna reported today that while the momentary crisis in the Austrian capital has passed, divisions of opinion at the highest levels still exist. All current activities and mutual attacks are fueled by deep-rooted nationalism and political fanaticism. The two main goals are (1) the old theory of complete annexation with Germany and (2) the continued maintenance of Austria's independence. Victory News today also revealed the following about the Austrian situation: "The Italian government's opposition to the major powers' joint intervention methods in Berlin has become increasingly firm. However, Mussolini's opposition to joint intervention by the powers does not indicate goodwill towards Germany, but rather because he deeply believes that intervention is useless. He has decided to act, not just talk." The attitude of the authorities in Paris remains as firm and suspicious as it has been in recent days. France's policy is to cooperate with both London and Rome to avoid the suspicion of hasty intervention. (National Telegraph, 30th)

Mrs. Dollfuss Arrives in Rome, Sees Children, and Cries Bitterly for Late Husband 32

Rome: Mrs. Dollfuss arrived here from Vienna at 0:45 PM today. Prime Minister Mussolini's wife led the Dollfuss children to the station to greet her. Local officials also came to welcome her. As soon as Mrs. Dollfuss saw her children, she thought of her late husband, embraced them, and cried. She also kissed Mrs. Mussolini. She then went to the Prime Minister's villa. Mussolini will arrive this evening. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Page 11

Commentary

The Problem of Employment After Graduation 33

The problem after university graduation is the problem of employment. Students study hard for several years, and once they reach graduation, who isn't happy and excited, expressing their satisfaction? But once they think of the pain of unemployment, who isn't worried and crying out loudly? According to the declaration issued by the Beiping University Students' Employment Movement Alliance and its letter to university graduates across the country, it is clear that the majority of university graduates are currently deeply troubled by unemployment and don't know what to do in the future. At this time of national crisis, we believe that it is a great loss to the country that these ambitious young people cannot contribute what they have learned to the nation. Therefore, for the sake of the country, appropriate relief should be provided as soon as possible so that each can develop their strengths, in accordance with the purpose of cultivating talent for the country. If the three points of President Wang's reply to the students' representatives' requests can be earnestly implemented, it would be a blessing for the unemployed students in general.

However, when we look back, since the abolition of the imperial examination system and the establishment of schools, the educators have never stopped thinking about the students' career prospects after graduation. However, the way of arranging employment has only been considered from the perspective of government offices, and society has often been alienated from and not very appreciative of these educated talents. Therefore, until today, scholars only know how to become officials and seek a living in the bureaucracy. In fact, the number of government officials in the country is limited, and the number of those who want to become officials to make a living is infinite. As a result, the political path is crowded, learning is not applied, and application is not learned, which has become a common ailment. Moreover, the ups and downs of officialdom are uncertain, and personnel changes are impermanent. Between one gain and one loss, promising young people often turn into social germs in an instant. This not only loses the original meaning of education but also becomes a furnace for destroying talent. This is the error of seeking employment exclusively in officialdom.

Then, should they abandon officialdom and seek employment in various state-run enterprises? But how many state-run enterprises can there be? Should they retreat further and seek employment in agriculture, industry, and commerce? It seems that agriculture, industry, and commerce have more uses and a wider scope and should be able to recruit a large number of talents to gradually improve their businesses. However, although we claim to be a country founded on agriculture, the methods of agricultural production and the relationship between land and population distribution make it difficult to accommodate specialized talents. Moreover, talents with specialized agricultural knowledge find it even more difficult to return to the countryside and relive the peasant life that is similar to primitive society. Therefore, the fact that agriculture is not a viable outlet for university students has already been proven and can be dismissed. In addition, the fields of industry and commerce seem to be most needed in today's world of industrial and commercial competition. However, China is not only affected by the economic panic but also subjected to various external pressures. Even relatively upwardly developing industries such as the textile industry cannot even maintain the status quo, let alone have room to accommodate new talents. Various other businesses are declining day by day and are difficult to develop for a while. Moreover, industry and commerce have their own personnel origins and a certain scope and value business experience, offer low compensation, and require a lot of work, which is incompatible with the ambitions of university students. As a result, the career path for university graduates is becoming narrower, and the unemployment problem is becoming more serious.

In the past, our country's education only focused on the cultivation of knowledge during the school period. However, whether this kind of cultivation is sufficient and whether it is practical, the school authorities have not deeply researched, and the educated themselves have no ability to choose. Therefore, whether knowledge can be applied to practice remains to be known only after future experimentation. During the school years, students are almost isolated from society. Once they leave school and enter society, they have a feeling of not knowing where to go. The education authorities cannot but bear their responsibility. Therefore, we advocate today that, on the one hand, the education authorities should be urged to work hard to eliminate long-standing malpractices and open up career paths for graduating youth, and on the other hand, the graduating students should also be cautious in their choice of careers. First, they must understand the current situation and whether they have appropriate knowledge and ability to promote a certain career, and whether they have a deep understanding of it. Second, most young people in school are ambitious but lack talent and often fail to deeply understand the facts. Once life presses in and the social economy is shaken, few can avoid being seriously hit. Therefore, after leaving school and encountering unemployment difficulties, they must have a spirit of enduring hardship, being able to suffer losses, being able to persevere, and not being tempted by external factors. With such efforts and struggles, there will be results in the future. Third, they must pay attention to small things. Promising young people in our country often become discouraged and depressed at the slightest setback. Once they achieve success, they forget their original mission. They should try to encourage themselves, start from small things, work hard, and not pursue distant goals. Individuals can get opportunities for training, and the country and nation can also benefit accordingly. Therefore, although they are in dire straits today, there is still great hope for the future.

Hindenburg's Health Deteriorates 34

Long-Suffering from Cystitis Leads to Weakness

Approaching Ancient Times, Fear He Will Not Recover

Much Speculation About His Successor as President

Neudeck: President Hindenburg has been suffering from cystitis for a long time. His condition worsened on Sunday night, and he is gradually failing. Doctors today expressed extreme concern about the president's life. This highly respected heroic statesman, whose life has exceeded that of the German Empire, was still able to receive guests and read official documents as usual until Monday. But since then, due to old age and prolonged illness, he has gradually become unsustainable and is feared he will not recover. The official statement said that President Hindenburg has been suffering from cystitis for many months, but since going to Neudeck for treatment, his condition has greatly improved. He was in slightly better spirits this morning. Although unwilling to be confined to his bed, he insisted on getting up for a short sit. According to the attending physician's bulletin at 12:25 this afternoon, "The President got up this morning and took tonics. He was quite interested in the surrounding environment. He went back to bed and fell asleep without chills or fever. His pulse was strong and slightly rapid." The German constitution stipulates that in the event of the President's death, the Chief Justice of the German Supreme Court will temporarily act as president. However, it is believed here that a cabinet meeting will be convened to temporarily hand over the presidential duties to Prime Minister Hitler, and General Goering, a confidant of Prime Minister Hitler, may serve as Deputy Prime Minister. President Hindenburg experienced the Franco-Prussian War in 1871 and witnessed the rise and fall of the German Empire. He was old and originally hoped to retire to Hanover to end his days. Unexpectedly, the European War broke out in 1914, and the German army had to fight France in the west and Russia in the east. Hindenburg was called out of retirement to lead the army in a fierce battle, defeating the Russian army and saving the German Empire. He then witnessed the defeat of the German army, the exile of Emperor Wilhelm, and the establishment of the republic, and then retired again. Unexpectedly, he was elected as President, and had to come out of retirement again to save the German Republic. (National Telegraph, 31st)

(Berlin): According to today's bulletin, the German President Hindenburg's unwellness is worrying. It is reported that he is suffering from weakness. Until the end of last week, the German President was still healthy, and he was still well yesterday, but he felt unwell at night and was quite weak. The German President is now eighty-seven years old, and he is old, so the doctors are quite anxious. However, they hope that his physical strength is good and that he will recover soon. At 12:25 this afternoon, four doctors signed and issued a bulletin, saying that President Hindenburg got up, ate a little breakfast, and paid attention to the people around him. Then he went to bed, and soon fell asleep again, without chills or fever, and his pulse was normal and stronger than before. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Another telegram: The German official news agency issued a notice this afternoon, saying that President Hindenburg's condition is now causing great anxiety. It is generally believed that if President Hindenburg passes away, the Duke of Brunswick, the son-in-law of the German former emperor, is the most promising successor. The Duke had planned to go to Japan to participate in the International Red Cross Conference, but due to the President's precarious condition, he has now abandoned the plan. (Reuters dispatch)

(Berlin): The news of President Hindenburg's critical illness has shocked the German people. There is much speculation about who will succeed Hindenburg as President. In addition to the Duke of Brunswick, the following are possible candidates: (1) General Mackensen, 85 years old, a famous general in the European War, (2) President Hindenburg's son, a large landowner and his father's advisor, (3) Chief of Staff of the Defense Forces, General Fritsch, (4) Prime Minister Hitler. According to the old constitution, the president must be elected by the German people. However, after Hitler took office as Prime Minister, the election law was amended, approved by President Hindenburg, and authorized the cabinet to act expediently. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

(Berlin): President Hindenburg's ill health is a cause for great concern. Prime Minister Hitler has convened an emergency meeting of all cabinet members. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

(Berlin): This afternoon, a high-ranking official told a Reuters reporter that President Hindenburg's condition must be considered serious and that precautions must be taken in case of the worst. According to reports, the German President joined the army in 1865 and participated in many battles. When the European War broke out, he was living in retirement in the wilderness, but he was soon appointed as the Commander-in-Chief of the Eastern Prussian Army. In 1916, he was appointed as the Chief of Staff until the end of the European War. After the death of German President Ebert in 1925, he was elected as President. On April 10, 1932, he was re-elected as the German head of state with a majority of six million votes. (Reuters dispatch, 31st)

Bulgaria Approves Pan-American Non-Aggression Pact 35

Sofia, Bulgaria: Newspapers report that the Argentine government has initiated a Pan-American Non-Aggression Pact and invited Bulgaria to join. It is reported that the Bulgarian government has decided to sign this pact. This pact was initiated by Argentine Foreign Minister Saavedra, and most American countries have expressed their support. Italy also approved it last December. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Italy and Bulgaria Establish Three Economic Agreements 36

Rome: Prime Minister Mussolini and Bulgarian representative Totu Gogalachov signed three economic agreements last night at the Palazzo Venezia: (1) A treaty of commerce and navigation with two lists of goods attached, specifying several major export goods and reducing import taxes in the other signatory country, (2) A veterinary convention stipulating sanitary regulations for livestock and meat trade between the two countries, and (3) A record of agreements establishing a mixed commission to promote trade and a sub-commission to set freight rates for the transportation of goods between the two countries. Up to now, Italy and Bulgaria have only exchanged notes stipulating the mutual application of the most-favored-nation clause. Since the signing of the above agreements, the economic relations between the two countries have been completely resolved. (Havas dispatch, 30th)

San Francisco Dockworkers' Strike Ends 37

Strike Continues at Chicago Stockyards

San Francisco: Twelve thousand dockworkers and five thousand sailors on the Pacific coast, who have been on strike for nearly two months, have resumed work this morning. In total, eight people have died since the strike began, and losses have amounted to two hundred million yuan. (Havas dispatch, 31st)

Chicago: News tonight indicates that there has been progress in the mediation of the stockyards strike. Since this news was released, the government has continued to purchase 5,000 head of cattle daily from the drought-stricken areas. However, the strike has not stopped, and the stockyards are still deserted. (National Telegraph, 31st)

Japan Appoints New Ambassadors to Colombia and Afghanistan 38

(United Press dispatch, 31st)

Weishi Autumn Harvest Submerged 39

Plague Outbreak in Northern Manchuria 43

(Beiping) Following the summer floods in various counties of the two provinces of Northern Manchuria, Jilin and Heilongjiang, a plague has broken out. In Qijia Village, Nongan County, Jilin Province, the plague began on July 5th. The residents of Aolongtai, located eighteen li northwest of Shangjiadian in the county, and Dapingqiao Village in the second district, are also severely affected by the plague. After Japanese doctor Sakamoto of Nongan County examined two corpses of plague victims, it was confirmed that they had indeed contracted the plague. The puppet authorities began taking preventive measures on July 1st, but unexpectedly, infectious diseases continued to break out in various counties of Northern Manchuria, with successive deaths increasing daily. According to statistics from various localities, the number of deaths has reached over 560 people. The lymph nodes in the necks and groins of those affected are swollen. Japanese engineer Ando of the puppet Fengtian Provincial Government has been investigating various areas of Northern Manchuria since July 12th and is planning to establish a plague investigation institute. Merchants and civilians passing through Tongliao to various parts of Southern Manchuria must undergo strict inspection in Tongliao before being allowed to pass. (31st Special Dispatch)

The Panchen Lama's Talk in Beiping 46

(Beiping) The Panchen Lama stated, "There are no fundamental problems regarding my return to Tibet. Since I have been in the Central Plains for a long time, the preparations are quite complex. I plan to go to Yimeng to chant scriptures after the PingSui Railway reopens, and then go to Qinghai to return to Tibet via a detour. I expect to travel around autumn and winter this year. If time is not sufficient, I may spend the winter at sea and set off next spring, which is also possible. The four northeastern provinces are adjacent to Ximeng. Because the four northeastern provinces have been occupied, Dongmeng has become a vassal of these four provinces. This is not the wish of the officials and people of Dongmeng. Reports claiming that unscrupulous Wang Gong are plotting collusion with Ximeng at the instigation of the Japanese, or even uniting with Outer Mongolia to pledge allegiance to Japan, are merely fantasies. I can say with certainty that this will not become a reality. The Japanese often claim that Inner Mongolia is attempting to brew an autonomous group, or that the Soviet Union has some kind of conspiracy regarding the entire Mongolian territory. However, the Chinese nation is a great nation united by the Han, Manchu, Mongol, Hui, and Tibetan ethnic groups, and cannot act alone. Otherwise, 'if the lips are gone, the teeth will be cold,' as the ancient saying goes. When I was stationed in Dongmeng and Ximeng in the past, my impression was that the Mongolians clearly knew that they were Chinese citizens, and they knew nothing else. Recently, after the establishment of the Inner Mongolia Autonomous Political Affairs Council, its purpose is to improve the lives of the Mongolians and build the area, with no other purposes. The various points reported by the Japanese are absolutely not true. The Tibetan people's inclination towards the interior has never waned. Since the news of my return to Tibet spread there, officials and people have cheered enthusiastically. Envoys welcoming me are constantly on the road. Representatives of the three major monasteries in the former Tibet are already on their way and will arrive soon. Qinghai and Tibet border the United Kingdom, so the relationship is difficult to sever immediately. I have known many important British figures for a long time. I believe that national rejuvenation and diplomatic relations must be clearly distinguished and cannot be confused. The Dalai Lama also based his claims on this, seeking the welfare of the country. Rumors that the Dalai Lama is training soldiers himself and serving as the commander-in-chief of the Tibetan army are inaccurate, because religion and politics cannot be mixed." (31st Special Dispatch)

Ministry of Finance Decides to Protect Shenxin Textile Mill 50

Kong Xiangxi's Reply to Wu Zhihui

(Nanjing) Kong Xiangxi's reply to Wu Zhihui stated, "When the Shenxin Textile Mill incident occurred, I was on my way. I tried to maintain it several times, and after returning, I conducted various investigations and consulted with President Wang of the Executive Yuan, the Economic Commission of the Ministry of Industry, and colleagues in Shanghai to carefully study and find ways to help. I also showed your opinions to Chairman Chiang, and I am even more grateful for your concern for national products and the maintenance of industry. After reading Mr. Zhou Danzhi's letter, I admire him deeply. The difficulty of returning to state-owned enterprises is evident in practice, as you said. Regarding the issue of government loans to maintain the mill, I have promised Mr. Rong to discuss it. When I first returned to Shanghai, Zhang Gongquan, Chen Guangfu, and others visited me. I immediately expressed that the government believes that the scale of the Shenxin Textile Mill is grand, its creation was difficult, and Mr. Rong's fighting spirit is rare in the industrial world of our country today. Moreover, its business is related to people's livelihood and is not just a matter of personal success or failure. At this critical moment, we should do our best to maintain it so that it can overcome difficulties. Since then, anyone who has questioned me about this matter has been told the same. Now that all parties know the government's intentions, they are no longer demanding from Mr. Rong, and Mr. Rong can also operate more flexibly and find his own path. As for the financial aspects in the future, if government assistance is necessary, we will do our best to find a way to live up to your expectations and will never allow it to stop, so as to curb the opportunity for the industry to grow. This is my intention for this case, and I believe it is the government's duty. However, our country is currently in a period of backward production and economic oppression. To compete with foreigners in the market, it seems that we must gradually improve in terms of technology and management, so that after spending less and achieving greater results, it will become more stable. I believe that you and Mr. Rong share the same feeling, and I deeply admire your insights and hopes. I would like to forward this intention, or it may be a key to the revival of Shenxin. (31st Special Dispatch)

(Nanjing) Chu Minyi said that the Shenxin Textile Mill had excessive debts in the past, making it difficult to continue. The government believed that it was related to the entire industry and had a significant impact on the market, so it was discussed at the Central Political Conference that the government should step in to maintain it. The Ministry of Industry and the Ministry of Finance investigated the matter and are currently planning it. Recently, Rong himself has gradually found a solution, so the government's efforts to maintain Rong's business are to spiritually ensure that creditors do not urge repayments, and materially allow Rong's factories to pay unified taxes on credit, so as to facilitate turnover. Because Rong's factories pay about 800,000 yuan in unified taxes each month, the government will provide relief. At most, it will need to allocate 3 to 4 million yuan, so this tax credit method will sufficiently relieve Rong's business of considerable difficulties. As for the reorganization plan, it will be temporarily shelved. (31st Special Dispatch)

Gold and Silver 66

London Gold Price: The London gold price remains at 138 shillings and a half pence today, the same as yesterday's price.

London Silver Bar: In the London silver market, the United States and India made slight purchases during the stable market conditions. China bought and then sold. The current price is 20 pence and 3125, up by 125. The futures price is 20 pence and 375, up by 0625.

New York Silver Bar: The silver market remains unremarkable.

Bombay Silver Bar: The Bombay silver market is calm today. The spot price is 56 rupees and 13 annas, and the August price is 56 rupees and 13, both unchanged. The September price rose by 1 anna to 56 rupees and 15 annas.

Exchange Rates 67

GBP/USD: The London foreign exchange market was sluggish this morning. The opening price for the GBP/USD exchange rate was 5.0375, the same as the closing price for yesterday's USD/GBP exchange rate. The price gradually fell before noon, and the price at noon was 5.036875, 0625 lower than the opening price. This price remained unchanged until 2:00 PM. One US dollar is equal to 3 shillings and 11 pence and 649 English gold.

GBP/FRF: The opening price was 76.40 francs. At 11:00 AM, it rose by 6 points to 76.46 francs, and there were no further changes.

USD/GBP: The New York foreign exchange market was lower by 125 this morning, at 5.03625. Prices did not change much before noon, but then fell by another 125 to 5.035.

Cotton and Wheat 68

US Cotton: The cotton market opened steadily. The October price was 1.0320, up 7 points from yesterday's close due to purchases by domestic counterparts, Europe, and the Far East. It fell slightly later. The most recent price is 1.0317. Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market was bought by many parties and futures traders, and there was some speculative selling later. The closing was stable. The July price for white Rochai cotton was 220.75 rupees, up 1.25 rupees.

British Cotton: The Liverpool cotton market opened steadily. At 1:00 PM, the October price rose by 5 points to 6.88.

British Wheat: The Liverpool wheat market opened lower today. At 1:00 PM, the October price was 5 shillings and 8 pence, half a penny lower than yesterday's close.

US Wheat: The wheat market opened lower due to weak news from Liverpool, but then rebounded slightly.

Rubber 69

London: The London rubber market was firm due to purchases by investors and speculators. The transaction price for the October-December period was 7.23125 pence, 0625 higher than yesterday.

New York: The rubber market opened firm, as the news from London was stronger. The opening price was 14.77, 12 points higher than yesterday's close. The market remained stable throughout the morning and prices trended upward.

Secretary-General of the Jiangxi Campaign Headquarters, Yang Yongtai, Lectures 84

The New Life Movement and the Four Cardinal Principles: Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame

Various parties have three questions related to the New Life Movement. First, China has many inherent virtues. Why does the New Life Movement specifically advocate "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame"? Isn't this focusing on one thing while neglecting others?

A General Review of Human Morality

(1) Morality Transcending Time and Space

(2) Morality Tied to Time and Space

(1) Private Morality... Morality of Society Under Familism

(2) Public Morality

A. Morality of Society Under the Ideal of Great Harmony

B. Morality of Society Under the Ideal of Universalism

C. Morality of Society Under Nationalism

Second, although "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" are a type of inherent Chinese social morality, they are actually plain and unremarkable, and an old remedy that has long been ineffective. They are not a special medicine imported from abroad. China's condition is very complicated. Can this old remedy be used as a panacea for saving the country?

(1) "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" are indeed a famous old remedy in China. However, in the past, has China ever taken the medicine according to the prescription? If the medicine was taken, it was not based on this prescription, or it was occasionally adopted while arbitrarily adding or subtracting ingredients, considering it an aid to other main prescriptions. Then, it cannot be concluded that this old remedy is ineffective. (2) "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" are indeed an inherent Chinese old remedy, not a special medicine invented by foreign countries. However, in various Western and Eastern countries under modern nationalism, the common medicine they use to maintain society, when analyzed, contains many components of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame." If foreign countries have this medicine without this prescription, then this ancient Chinese prescription is even more worthy of attention.

(3) Whether "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" can be used as a panacea for saving the country should be determined by whether the medicine is suitable for the illness. Although China's current condition is very complicated, tracing the source of the disease, it is indeed mostly caused by a lack of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame." Therefore, our main prescription should only emphasize the four ingredients of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame." Long-term adherence is necessary, and arbitrary addition or subtraction is not allowed, especially mixing Chinese and Western medicines.

Third, why must "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" be expressed in daily life, in food, clothing, housing, and transportation? This requires the virtues of inner cultivation. If we only focus on the external expression of form, wouldn't it be close to superficiality and easily lead to hypocrisy?

In my previous speech, I used "Revolution First Revolutionizes the Heart, Political Reform First Changes Customs" as the title. In thousands of words, everything I said was a wedge for the New Life Movement, a general explanation of why we should do the New Life Movement. Regarding the content and importance of the New Life Movement, Chairman Chiang Kai-shek's speeches, in addition to being printed into booklets, also personally wrote the Outline of the New Life Movement and Essentials for the New Life, providing a systematic explanation that is both detailed and comprehensive. There is no need for me to add unnecessary details. After this movement occurred, it spread like wildfire, and the whole country responded. It can be seen that it is clearly appropriate for the people's hearts and deeply aligns with the consistent demands of the people. There is also no need to make further inferences. However, summarizing the comments from various parties, there are still several related questions that inevitably arise. Although the views cannot be completely identical, they are all well-intentioned discussions and not fundamental disapprovals. Now, taking this opportunity, I will answer the following three questions separately, making a "comment on the comments": First, China has many inherent virtues. Why does the New Life Movement specifically advocate "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame"? Isn't this focusing on one thing while neglecting others?

Second, although "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" are a type of inherent Chinese social morality, they are actually plain and unremarkable, and an old remedy that has long been ineffective. They are not a special medicine imported from abroad. China's condition is very complicated. Can this old remedy be used as a panacea for saving the country? Third, why must "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" be expressed in daily life, in "food, clothing, housing, and transportation"? This requires the virtues of inner cultivation. If we only focus on the external expression of form, wouldn't it be close to superficiality and easily lead to hypocrisy?

The above three questions have been successively raised by various parties since the New Life Movement occurred. The following answers them one by one in order.

First, China has many inherent virtues. Why does the New Life Movement specifically advocate "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame"? Isn't this focusing on one thing while neglecting others?

China indeed has many inherent virtues. Confucius and Mencius spoke of "Wisdom, Benevolence, and Courage," calling them the three universally recognized virtues, setting them as the highest goals to strive for. They also spoke of the five relationships and the five constants. The five relationships are "affection between father and son, righteousness between ruler and subject, distinction between husband and wife, order between elder and younger, and trust between friends." The five constants are "benevolence, righteousness, propriety, wisdom, and trustworthiness." There was no specific discussion of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame." In the time of Confucius and Mencius, the four characters "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" had not yet been combined into a single term. The "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" spoken of after the Han and Song dynasties were also mentioned alongside the eight characters "Filial piety, Brotherly love, Loyalty, and Trustworthiness." "Filial piety, Brotherly love, Loyalty, and Trustworthiness" were still ranked ahead of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame," and their special importance was not highlighted. Even Sun Yat-sen, in his Nationalism, said that we must restore the inherent morality of the Chinese nation. First is loyalty and filial piety, second is benevolence and love, third is trustworthiness and righteousness, and fourth is peace. (Some say that these are the eight virtues, which is actually incorrect. We can only say that loyalty and filial piety are one virtue, benevolence and love are one virtue, trustworthiness and righteousness are one virtue, and peace is one virtue, which together are four virtues.) There was also no specific discussion of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame." It can be seen that the Chinese morality advocated by past sages has various forms, all of which should be given equal importance. Why does Chairman Chiang Kai-shek specifically advocate "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" in the New Life Movement? Isn't this focusing on one thing while neglecting others? To understand this principle, we must first classify all human morality and conduct a review based on its nature. For the sake of convenient explanation, I want to classify it into a simple table to make it easy to understand at a glance. Roughly, all human morality can be broadly divided into two categories: one that transcends time and space and one that is tied to time and space. Morality that is tied to time and space can be further divided into two types: private morality and public morality. Private morality is the morality most revered by society under familism. Public morality can be further divided into three types: (1) the morality most revered by society under nationalism, (2) the morality most revered by society under universalism, and (3) the morality most revered by society under the ideal of great harmony. Understanding these types of morality and distinguishing the nature of these moralities, then the position of "Propriety, Justice, Integrity, and Shame" among all kinds of morality and its importance in Chinese society today will become self-evident without detailed explanation.

(1) Morality That Transcends Time and Space

In my view, the "Wisdom, Benevolence, and Courage" spoken of by our ancient sages and virtuous men are the highest morality of humankind that transcends time and region. Every nation, every country, or every religion should take this as the ultimate standard, practicing it for centuries without confusion and applying it to all corners of the world without error. The "Wisdom, Benevolence, and Courage" of Confucianism are like the "Precepts, Concentration, and Wisdom" of Buddhism. "Wisdom" is intelligence, and the meaning of "Concentration" is similar to "Benevolence." Buddhism emphasizes cultivation to achieve concentration. After concentration, there is nothing in the heart, not a single thought arises, like a bright mirror hanging high, capable of illuminating all phenomena, which is the result of seeing one's own nature. The word "Benevolence" in Confucianism, from the perspective of the function of "Benevolence," certainly has many aspects, but from the perspective of the essence of "Benevolence," it is the same principle as the "Concentration" of Buddhism. Yan Hui, Confucius's first major disciple, although very young, was the earliest to hear the Tao. His greatest strength was that "his heart did not deviate from Benevolence for three months." This is the effort of "Concentration," which he did very thoroughly. That is, the Great Learning says, "Knowing where to rest, you can have concentration; with concentration, you can be tranquil; with tranquility, you can be at peace; with peace, you can deliberate; with deliberation, you can achieve." This kind of effort of concentration means that the heart does not move recklessly, human desires are completely cleansed, and the principles of Heaven are fully preserved. Only Yan Hui could achieve this step, so he could become Confucius's most outstanding disciple. "Precepts" are similar to "Courage." Precepts are adhering to precepts. People must have things they will not do before they can have things they can do. At any time when one resolutely does not do something or resolutely does something, one must first make a determination. To make a determination, one must have a kind of courage. "Wisdom, Benevolence, and Courage" and "Precepts, Concentration, and Wisdom," although different on the surface, are actually no different in the effort of cultivation in essence. They are both the highest and most supreme morality that transcends time and space. (To be continued)

A Person from the Northeast Talks About the Intensification of the Russo-Japanese Conflict 85

Russian Planes Reconnoiter Fujin, Hulin, Raohe and Other Counties

Russian Artillery Fires at Puppet Military District from Sanjiangkou Fortress

Japanese Use Confiscated Civilian Guns to Prepare for Conscription

According to people from Harbin, war clouds are gathering over Northeast China, with a sense of imminent outbreak. Therefore, the news of the Russo-Japanese war is spreading in various places in the Northeast, causing people to panic. The situation is especially serious in Harbin. Regarding the military preparations of both sides, on July 15, two Soviet Russian planes suddenly flew over the skies of Fujin, Hulin, Raohe, and other counties to scout the deployment of Japanese and puppet troops and military industrial facilities. The Soviet Russians have repeatedly fired artillery across the river at the puppet military district from the Sanjiangkou Fortress to show their threat. The Soviet Russians have also built fortifications along the border. Every night, searchlights begin to emit beams of light that are dazzling, like fire dragons, visible from across the river. On the Japanese and puppet side, Harbin has been under undeclared martial law recently, and travelers are being heavily inspected. There are also rumors that the Russo-Japanese War is about to begin, and the market is particularly sluggish. In order to prevent unforeseen circumstances, the Japanese and puppet authorities have been strictly interrogating travelers, pedestrians on the streets, and in hotels. It is reported that more than 50 young national salvation activists have been arrested and brutally killed. In order to expand military construction, the Japanese army has established eight major bureaus to handle civil engineering matters, such as repairing airfields, building military roads, and constructing border fortifications. These are all handled exclusively by the eight major bureaus and completely controlled by the Japanese. The Japanese military authorities are also forcing the puppet Ministry of Military Affairs to actively conscript soldiers, who are completely trained by the Japanese. All officers are filled by the Japanese. The civilian guns confiscated from various places this spring will be issued to the newly conscripted soldiers. (Northeast News Agency)

Songjiang 86

Changes in the Collection of Tobacco and Alcohol License Tax

The tobacco and alcohol license tax used to be collected by the Ministry of Finance. Since the financial conference decided to abolish excessive taxes in various provinces, cities, and counties to alleviate the people's suffering, the tobacco and alcohol license tax was transferred to the collection of each province and city as a compensation for the cancellation of excessive taxes. The licenses are still printed and issued by the Ministry of Finance to all provinces to be forwarded to the finance departments for compliance. Now, the county government received instructions from the finance department that the tobacco and alcohol license tax has been directly collected by this province since July 1st. Gu Baoyu has been appointed as the director and Pan Xiangxin as the deputy director to assist in the process. It is rumored that a Mr. Zhu from Pinghu has contracted the tax amount to be collected in this county, but he has not yet come to Songjiang.

Suzhou Reporters' Games Open Today 87

The Suzhou News Reporters' Games, initiated by reporters from various newspapers in Suzhou, has been fully prepared and is scheduled to open at 2:00 PM today (the 1st). The location is the public stadium. Various circles have donated more than 100 prizes. Zhao Dihua, the director of the Finance Department, sent a banner with the words "May the Athletes Charge Against the Wind". The Department of Civil Affairs and the Shanghai Municipal Government have also donated prizes. There are 16 sports events in total. County Magistrate Wu Qiyun is specially invited to be the chairman of the conference, and Ms. Xu Xianmin, the wife of former Wu County Magistrate Peng Guoyan, is invited to present the awards. It is estimated that more than 40 athletes will participate.

Plotting to Kill Her Husband, She Receives Death Penalty 88

Wang Jinshan, the temple keeper of Maoshan Temple in Qian Wanli Bridge, had a wife, Wang Pan, who had an affair with her son-in-law, Chen Wanquan. In April of this year, Wang Pan and Chen Wanquan conspired to kill Wang Jinshan and threw his body into the river. After the discovery, Wang Pan and Chen Wanquan were arrested one after another. They were escorted by the Public Security Bureau to the local court for trial. The local court has completed the trial and announced the verdict at 10:00 AM yesterday (the 31st). Wang Pan and Chen Wanquan committed murder and were sentenced to death.

Two Robberies Near Taihu Lake in One Night 89

In Taili Township, Xishan, Dongting, which belongs to the county, at around 10:00 PM on the 30th, eight or nine lake bandits suddenly came to the home of farmer Gu Renshan. Each held guns and broke down the door to rob arbitrarily. They robbed 92 silver dollars and clothes and other items and fled. As they left, they opened fire and injured the leg of the victim Gu Renshan. It turned out that after robbing the Gu family, the bandits took a boat and went to rob a pig transport ship they encountered on the way near Taihu Lake. Since there was no silver, they only robbed a few clothes and four large pigs and fled towards Yuanshan.

Raping a Young Girl, He is Sentenced to Eight Years 90

Lu Genhu, who lives at No. 76 Furenfang Alley, raped 13-year-old Ma Wenhui on the 3rd of this month. Ma reported it to the police station, and Lu Genhu was arrested and escorted to the local court for trial. The local court issued a verdict yesterday (the 31st), sentencing Lu Genhu to eight years of imprisonment for raping a girl under the age of sixteen.

Wuxi Telegraphs for Suspension of Autumn Cocoon Improvement Fee 91

The Jiangsu Construction Department, in order to forcibly improve the silkworm industry in this province, strictly implemented silkworm seed control. In the spring cocoon season of this year, a improvement fee of three silver dollars was collected for each dan of dry cocoons. From the autumn cocoon season, twelve dollars must be paid to improve the silkworm and mulberry business. Now that the spring cocoon season has passed, the autumn cocoon season is approaching. Cocoon merchants in various places have protested against this method. For example, the Wujin and Yixing Cocoon Industry Associations, as well as various public groups such as the agricultural, commercial, and educational associations, all believe that the control method is close to excessive taxation, which harms farmers and is not conducive to business, and there is no hope of improving the business. They have successively telegraphed to the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, the Ministry of Industry, and Chairman Chiang of the Nanchang Campaign Headquarters, requesting orders to stop it. The Wuxi Silk Factory Association also stated that the silk industry is declining, the countryside is bankrupt, and there is a severe drought. Yesterday, they also telegraphed the provincial department to stop collecting this improvement fee for this autumn cocoon season.

Jiangsu Provincial Government to Issue Huge Public Bonds 92

The Jiangsu Provincial Government, due to a large budget deficit and the urgent need to repay old public bonds, decided to issue 30 million yuan in public bonds with a term of 20 years and an annual interest rate of 7%. It will use 1.8 million yuan of salt tax surcharges, 1 million yuan of deed tax, and 300,000 yuan of land tax per year, totaling 3.1 million yuan, as collateral. The purpose is to use 6 million yuan to repay the principal and interest owed to various banks, 9 million yuan to repay old public bonds, 8.5 million yuan for the cost of guiding the Huai River into the sea, and 6.5 million yuan for the cost of dredging the new canal. It has been submitted to the Executive Yuan for review. Once approved, it will be prepared for issuance.

Summer Bamboo Shoots and Magnolias in Full Bloom 93

The town has never produced mountain bamboo shoots. There are only bamboo shoots in the bamboo garden, commonly known as Duyuan bamboo shoots. Their production time is within April and May, and it has not been heard that bamboo shoots are produced in the autumn season of July. Yesterday, there was news from the countryside that Poji bamboo, Yan bamboo, and May bamboo in bamboo gardens everywhere suddenly produced bamboo shoots, which were fatter and larger than the bamboo shoots in April and May. A large amount of goods were produced, and some were sold in the countryside and towns for about 100 cash per catty, but they were not fresh. Also, the magnolia flowers of Yin Guanqing's house under the Daxia Rainbow Bridge in the city suddenly contained buds and bloomed, just like the flowers that bloomed in February. This is specially recorded for the study of botanists.

Before long, a strong wind blew, and in Yeqiao, Sitou, Xizhang, Tangtou, Changanqiao and other places in the fifth district of the northern countryside, from 2:05 PM, hailstones and heavy rain fell together. The large hailstones were like chicken eggs, and the small ones were like copper coins. The rice seedlings in the fields in that area were slightly damaged. It stopped after half an hour, with about half an inch of hail and one and a half inches of rain. Also, in Yuqi, Qianzhou, Beiqifang, and other places in the ninth district, there were also more than two inches of rain. The houses of Guo Achuan's family in Jinyiaqiao, Area 62 of this district, were struck by lightning and burned down. Page 13

The City Grain Committee Discussed Aiding Rice Prices Yesterday 102

Resolved to Restrict Rice Prices and Dredge Rice Sources

Ordered that Rice Inventory Be Surveyed Before Ordering Foreign Rice

According to the Central News Agency, the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau's Grain Committee held its 42nd regular meeting at the Cuixiutang in the City Temple at 1:00 PM yesterday. The meeting reported on the recent food situation in the city and discussed ways to suppress rice prices. The meeting adjourned at approximately 4:00 PM. The details of the meeting are as follows:

Committee Members Present 103

The committee members present were Chen Jixi, Yao Yuanjun, Zhou Minggang, Zhang Binghui, Lin Dun, Yu Zixiang, Wu Juenong, Huang Yinong (deputized by Cheng Fengyun), Lu Wenshao, Jiang Shizhi, Gu Xinyi, Wu Huanru, Cai Yukun, Zhu Zixiang, Yan Xiaoquan, Sun Yongyi, Huang Zune, and seventeen others.

Meeting Details 104

Yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, all the committee members arrived on time and the meeting began. Chairman Zhang Binghui and recorder Zhou Minggang performed the formalities. First, the chairman reported on the recent soaring rice prices. Then, the committee members expressed their opinions and began to discuss and decide on three relief measures.

Chairman's Report 105

Chairman Zhang Binghui reported, briefly stating: (1) Since the 41st regular meeting of this committee, there have been no important proposals, so it has been regrettable that the meeting has not been held for a long time. Now that it is summer, the weather is arid and various places have reported disasters, which will inevitably affect the autumn harvest. Since January, rice prices in the city have soared by more than three yuan per stone. The future of the people's food is truly worrying. However, since the rice industry restricted rice prices and timely rains fell frequently, rice prices have gradually declined. However, it is feared that if the weather is dry again, the amount of rainfall will not be much, and the source will be reduced, and panic will occur again, which is difficult to say. The Social Bureau has repeatedly issued instructions from the municipal government to restrict the sharp rise in rice prices and to dredge rice sources to maintain the people's food. This committee is the only advisory body for the city's food problem. Please ask the committee members to express their opinions and seek solutions together. The city's food future truly depends on it. (2) The letter No. 6324 from the Social Bureau stated that according to the presentation of the City Rice Trade Association, rice is related to people's livelihoods, and they requested serious attention. They ordered that it be properly reviewed and reported. The original text has been issued to each committee member and is requested to be discussed together as a basis for reply. (The original text has been seen in the previous newspaper and is omitted)

Committee Members' Statements 106

After the chairman's report, Committee Member Gu Xinyi rose to report, briefly stating: Since the rise in rice prices, the Rice Industry Association has considered ordering foreign rice to suppress rice prices, but because various parties have failed to express their sympathy, this proposal has been automatically withdrawn. Committee Member Wu Huanru reported, briefly stating: The rice-producing areas this year have indeed been affected by the drought, and the harvest has been reduced. When I attended the temporary meeting of the Executive Yuan, there was a discussion on prevention beforehand and remedies afterward. I believe that the current food may not rise too much, to what extent, but when the next harvest season, there may be a risk of rising. Therefore, ordering foreign rice seems feasible, but the method should be discussed. Committee Member Lu Wenshao reported, briefly stating: I think that ordering foreign rice should be considered carefully. It is not appropriate for rice to be expensive, but it is also enough to hurt farmers for rice to be cheap. The rice industry has already expressed this. I believe that the price of old rice should be restricted, and the price of new rice may be slightly increased. Other committee members also expressed their opinions, which are omitted here.

Agreed Upon Methods 107

After the reports from each committee member, the discussion of the proposed motions began. (1) Zhang Binghui proposed that due to the recent drought and impending famine, and the soaring rice prices in the city, a method should be devised to regulate the market to benefit the people's food supply. (2) Zhang Binghui proposed that the rice industry is considering purchasing foreign rice to prepare for famine. Should this be done, or should domestic rice be purchased from Hunan, Anhui, and other provinces first? Please discuss. (3) The Social Affairs Bureau submitted a proposal regarding the opinions of the rice industry on the rice supply, requesting a review and report for approval and implementation. The following methods were decided upon for the above three cases: (1) Rice prices should be limited, with a maximum price of thirteen yuan, and corresponding adjustments for lower grades. (2) Channels should be opened, and in addition to the rice merchants taking responsibility, the municipal government should consult with transportation authorities to facilitate the transportation of rice as quickly as possible. (3) Regarding the purchase of foreign rice, a survey of rice reserves in various regions should be conducted first. If necessary, rice merchants should purchase 500,000 shi of foreign rice on a forward contract. If losses occur in the future, the government will guarantee them and exempt import duties. If prices rise extremely high, in addition to paying import duties, the price of foreign rice will be restricted to stabilize the market. Detailed measures will be drafted by the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau and submitted to the Municipal Government, which will then consult with the governments of Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces and jointly submit them to the central government for approval.

District Farmers' Associations Met Yesterday 108

Discussing Disaster Relief Measures for Agricultural Disasters

The Municipal Farmers' Association convened a meeting of various district farmers' associations yesterday afternoon to discuss disaster relief measures for agricultural disasters. The details are recorded below:

Attending Representatives: Lu Dong of Gaoqiao District, Liu Zhaoxing of Wusong District, Gu Jinqing and Zhuang Yaocong of Fahua District, Wu Ruzhang of Caojing District, Hu Yingchun of Lixing District, Hu Zhusan of Yang'en District, Qu Xing of Gaohang District, Wang Hui of Tangqiao District, Xu Baoming of Yangjing District, Gu Tongchun of Pusong District, Shen Wenbin, Tang Guanchun, and He Ruiren of Zhabei District, Xing Guxiang of Yinxiang District, Hou Shizhang of Pengpu District, Pan Rongting and Zhu Hexiang of Huna District, and more than twenty others.

Reports from Each District: 1. Yu Zhenhui, Executive Director of the Municipal Farmers' Association, reported on the purpose of the discussion. (1) The implementation status of each district after the Municipal Government allocated funds. (2) Whether each district still needs water pumping. (3) Reimbursement of expenses and settlement of advance payments. 2. Lu Dong, representative of Gaoqiao District, reported that although the water pumps had been received for several days, they had not yet been put into operation because the length of the water pipes needed to be at least 60 feet and must wait for the decision of the Social Affairs Bureau before ordering from Shenchang Foreign Firm. The condition of the farmland requires water urgently. 3. Liu Zhaoxing, representative of Wusong District Farmers' Association, reported that the situation in Wusong is different from other districts due to the tidal water. Water pumping was in progress when there was timely rainfall, so manpower is no longer needed. The machinery was borrowed and the expenses advanced have reached more than one hundred yuan. 4. Wu Ruzhang, representative of Caojing District, reported that the district mainly grows edamame beans and less rice. Because the rivers are not interconnected, more machines are needed. 5. Hu Yingchun of Lixing District reported that the two heavy rains did not reach the area. The machines started pumping water yesterday, and the fuel is only enough for two days. The machines should be preserved for future needs. 6. Hu Zhusan of Yangsi District reported that the district had four or five rainfalls, but they were not significant. 7. Qu Xing of Gaohang District reported that the several heavy rains did not reach Gaohang, Gaoqiao, and Lixing. Although the machine is large, the amount of water pumped is not much, and the expenses advanced have reached more than one hundred yuan. 8. Wang Hui of Tangqiao District reported that one-third of all small rivers have been irrigated. The pumping started on the 6th, but the rainfall was scarce. Whether the machine is needed depends on the situation after the minor tide. 9. Gu Tongchun of Pusong District reported that the assigned machine could not pump water, so another machine was rented. There are a total of six dams, costing about one hundred and fifty yuan. Not only is the machine still needed, but it would be best to get a few more. 10. Shen Wenbin of Zhabei District reported that the machine is located in Yanjiabang, and the exact cost has not been determined. The need for water is no less than other districts. 11. Xing Guxiang of Yinxiang District reported that the district received three inches of rainfall and temporarily does not need water pumping. 12. Hou Shizhang of Pengpu District reported that at the beginning, fire engines were used to pump water for six days, providing more than ten yuan per day, which was not very beneficial. The machine has not yet been installed, and the need is gone due to the influence of the tide, and the expenses are high. 13. Zhuang Yaoming of Fahua District reported that the southern part of Fahua District suffered more severely. The northwest part has the Wusong River for irrigation. The main crops are cotton, beans, and vegetables. The demand for water for vegetables is high every day, and he requested that efforts be made to provide relief. 14. Pan Rongting of Huna District reported that the dam is in Shihui Port. The machine started pumping water on the 6th, but the horses are too small and not effective. Although the fire engine came, it was not used. The tide was blocked by the dam, which increased the inconvenience. The account is opened, please find a way to allocate it. 15. Xu Baoming of Yangjing District reported that the machine has not been received. There is no major problem along the shore because of the high tide. The disaster situation is serious from Qinci Yangdian to the junction of Gaohang and Nanhui. The Huacao Lian is dry for a long time, and fundamental solutions can be permanently effective.

Discussion Methods 109

(1) Request the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to allocate the funds advanced by each district for drought prevention in July. (2) The Municipal Farmers' Association will notify each district (such as Zhenru, Lixing, Tangqiao) to prepare a final account of drought prevention expenses for July within three days beyond the deadline and forward it. (3) If any district needs to continue pumping water in the future, the expenses should be allocated as requested. (4) Request the Municipal Government to specially deposit funds for drought prevention and surplus funds for urgent needs for drought prevention and treatment.

The Municipal Bureau of Finance Commences Collection of This Year's Early-Term Field Tax 110

Deadline for Completion within Two Months

Overdue Surcharge for Late Payment

The Municipal Bureau of Finance has scheduled the commencement of the collection of the early-term field tax for this year on August 1. The announcement is copied below: It is found that the field tax in this city has always been collected by converting the original busy transport at a discounted price. Subsequently, the "Silver Yuan Collection of Field Tax and Arrangement of Additional Field Tax" promulgated by the Ministry of Finance was followed, and starting in 1934, the original name of busy transport was abolished and collectively called field tax, which was divided into two items: regular tax and surtax. The original tax amount was still converted into silver yuan per mu, and collected in two terms, early and late. The original additional items collected were all incorporated into the surtax for internal calculation, and collected together with the regular tax at an average rate. If the surtax exceeded the regular tax, it was reduced separately to not exceed the regular tax. It has been submitted to the Municipal Government and forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for approval. All early-term field taxes for 1934 are now scheduled to be collected on August 1 of this year. In the case of the autumn disaster exemption for 1933, 20% should be allowed for Wuusong and Yinxing Districts, 15% for Yinxiang District, 10% for Gaohang, Lixing, and Yangsi Districts, and 0.5% for Zhenru and Jiangwan Districts. The remaining districts will still be collected according to the fixed amount and detailed in the license. The deadline for completing this term's field tax is two months from the date of collection, deducted to September 30 of this year. Those who have not completed payment by the deadline will be charged an additional 10% for late payment. An additional two months will be continued, deducted to November 30 of this year. Those who still have not completed payment by the deadline will be charged an additional 10% to show late payment. In addition to reporting to the Municipal Government for record and separately issuing letters, it is appropriate to issue a notice and announcement, so that everyone is aware of it and must go to the counter to complete payment within the time limit, obtain a license and settle down, and do not delay. This announcement.

The 6% British Gold Loan is Printed and Will Be Exchanged Starting Today 116

Divided into Three Types: 50 Pounds, 100 Pounds, and 1,000 Pounds

Managed by the Central and Other Four Banks for Principal and Interest Repayment

Xinsheng News Agency reports that the Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Railways of the National Government issued a 6% British Gold Gengkuan Loan of 1.5 million pounds in 1934 for the completion of the Guangdong-Hankou Railway. The Foundation Management Committee has been established and is underwritten by the Central, China, Communications, and HSBC Banks, which are responsible for the repayment of principal and interest. Now the loan tickets have been printed and handed over by the Ministry of Finance to the four banks that underwrote it. Starting today, the loan tickets will be exchanged based on the reservation certificates, divided into three types: 50 pounds, 100 pounds, and 1,000 pounds. January 1, 1935, is the date for the first principal repayment. After that, principal will be repaid every six months in 25 installments until January 1, 1947, when the principal and interest will be fully repaid. The four banks that underwrote the loan have formally announced the underwriting and are responsible for the repayment of principal and interest.
